name:E‚Äçp‚Äçi‚Äçj
info:Deluxe Queen Room
info:Stayed in January 2022
info:Solo travelers
info:20 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 17, 2022
msg:Service was good. I did not realise I needed to take a Covid test on arrival, but there was a hospital behind the hotel and they showed me where to go. A bit of a hassle, but it was taken care of quickly and I was then allowed into the room. The facilities are really good in this hotel. The gym is one of the better ones I have seen in a hotel. It is large and has quite a lot of equipment. There is also a pilates studio connected to the gym. There is an outdoor pool (although closed now as it is too cold) as well as a sauna, though this was also closed. The hotel is very close to some great restaurants (Blue Frog, Petit Chateau, Brownstone Tapas & Bar) and these were just in front. There were more local restaurants around the corner, but many choices all within walking distance. The cleaners were very kind and accommodating. The staff in general were very helpful and very attentive. It is about a 30 to 40 minute walk to the Oriental Pearl Tower, with many restaurants and places to see between the hotel and the financial area. I normally stay in the Jing'an area, but I would not hesitate to stay here again.

name:L‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçj‚Äçi‚Äçe
info:Deluxe Queen Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:3 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted March 9, 2024
msg:I was traveling alone and stayed at this hotel for one night. The location is about 10 minutes walk from Century Avenue Station. There are many commercial facilities and restaurants nearby, making it very lively.
When making the reservation, I requested a higher floor with a nice view if possible, and they arranged a place on the 36th floor with a great view. I was surprised that they could provide such a good room even though I was traveling alone for one night!
The rooms are spacious and the beds are big and clean, so you can spend a comfortable time. Although a certain amount of equipment and amenities are available, there are some items such as toothbrushes and combs that are not provided. For this, you can contact the dedicated number and they will help you, so if you forget it, you will need to use it. The windows are very large and you can enjoy the scenery from almost the entire surface. Although the view was like the one in the photo, it was still the lowest-ranked room with a queen bed.
There are many services available, and if you call the special dial from inside your room, you can do anything from meal service to taxi or limousine arrangements.

When it comes to disappointing points, the first one is the ease of use and speed of Wi-Fi. Wi-Fi is available throughout the hotel, not in each room. I was able to connect via SMS using my smartphone, but I could not connect to the internet at all. Most of the apps, including SNS, were not updated, and I had no choice but to use a borrowed pocket Wi-Fi.
Also, as mentioned above, some of the amenities that most guests would use are not provided, and it takes a lot of effort and time to call a dedicated number to request them. In that case, I feel that it would be faster to install it in the room. This may be due to the cost or the ingenuity of a long-established hotel, but I personally wish they provided toothbrushes and toothpaste.

Overall, it was a luxurious experience at a low price. I would like to use it again the next time I visit!
